\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00671}00671 \textcolor{comment}{// This is used by Settings to store persistent data while reducing allocation count.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00672}00672 \textcolor{comment}{// We store the chunk size first, and align the final size on 4 bytes boundaries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00673}00673 \textcolor{comment}{// The tedious/zealous amount of casting is to avoid -\/Wcast-\/align warnings.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00696}00696 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00697}00697 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawList: Helper function to calculate a circle's segment count given its radius and a "{}maximum error"{} value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00698}00698 \textcolor{comment}{// Estimation of number of circle segment based on error is derived using method described in https://stackoverflow.com/a/2244088/15194693}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00699}00699 \textcolor{comment}{// Number of segments (N) is calculated using equation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00700}00700 \textcolor{comment}{//   N = ceil ( pi / acos(1 -\/ error / r) )     where r > 0, error <= r}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00701}00701 \textcolor{comment}{// Our equation is significantly simpler that one in the post thanks for choosing segment that is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00702}00702 \textcolor{comment}{// perpendicular to X axis. Follow steps in the article from this starting condition and you will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00703}00703 \textcolor{comment}{// will get this result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00704}00704 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00705}00705 \textcolor{comment}{// Rendering circles with an odd number of segments, while mathematically correct will produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00706}00706 \textcolor{comment}{// asymmetrical results on the raster grid. Therefore we're rounding N to next even number (7-\/>8, 8-\/>8, 9-\/>10 etc.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00707}00707 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00708}00708 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_ROUNDUP\_TO\_EVEN(\_V)                                  ((((\_V) + 1) / 2) * 2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00709}00709 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MIN                     4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00710}00710 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MAX                     512}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00711}00711 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC(\_RAD,\_MAXERROR)    ImClamp(IM\_ROUNDUP\_TO\_EVEN((int)ImCeil(IM\_PI / ImAcos(1 -\/ ImMin((\_MAXERROR), (\_RAD)) / (\_RAD)))), IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MIN, IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MAX)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00712}00712 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00713}00713 \textcolor{comment}{// Raw equation from IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC rewritten for 'r' and 'error'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00714}00714 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC\_R(\_N,\_MAXERROR)    ((\_MAXERROR) / (1 -\/ ImCos(IM\_PI / ImMax((float)(\_N), IM\_PI))))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00715}00715 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC\_ERROR(\_N,\_RAD)     ((1 -\/ ImCos(IM\_PI / ImMax((float)(\_N), IM\_PI))) / (\_RAD))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00716}00716 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00717}00717 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawList: Lookup table size for adaptive arc drawing, cover full circle.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui__internal_8h_source_l00720}00720 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
